<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вос-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vos-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспитать.html>воспита́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vospitátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспитывать.html>воспи́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bring up, to rear, to educate</li>
<li>to educate, to train <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">somebody to be somebody</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<li>to foster, to cultivate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воспитать.html>воспита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:родина.html>ро́дине</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vospitátʹ</b> v rebjónke ljubóvʹ k ródine</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring up a child to love its country</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспитать.html>воспита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vospitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспитывать.html>воспи́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vospítyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспитать.html>воспита́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bring up, to rear, to educate</li>
<li>to educate, to train <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">somebody to be somebody</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воспитывать.html>воспи́тывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:педагог.html>педаго́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vospítyvatʹ</b> iz kovó-libo pedagóga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to train somebody to be a teacher</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to foster, to cultivate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воспитывать.html>воспи́тывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:родина.html>ро́дине</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vospítyvatʹ</b> v rebjónke ljubóvʹ k ródine</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring up a child to love its country</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вос-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vos-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-по́лнить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-pólnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>to fill in, to supply

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восполнить.html>воспо́лнить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробел.html>пробе́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ниях</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vospólnitʹ</b> probély v svoíx znánijax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fill in the gaps in one's knowledge</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восполнить.html>воспо́лнить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:потеря.html>поте́ри</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vospólnitʹ</b> potéri</i> ― <span class="e-translation">recoup one's losses</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to make up <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восполнить.html>воспо́лнить</a></b> что́-либо че́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vospólnitʹ</b> štó-libo čém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make up for smth with smth</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***воспользоваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воспользоваться.html>воспо́льзоваться</a> (2610)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вос-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vos-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пользовать.html>по́льзовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pólʹzovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспользоваться.html>воспо́льзоваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vospólʹzovatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пользоваться.html>по́льзоваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to avail oneself (of something), to make use, to profit (from), to take advantage (of), to seize (an opportunity)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>вос<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>по́ль<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 2a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>вос-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-польз-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ова</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воспоминание.html>воспомина́ние</a> (1447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспоминание.html>воспомина́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vospominánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспоминание.html>воспомина́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспоминание.html>воспомина́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспоминание.html>воспомина́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>memory, remembrance, recollection</li>
<li><i>(plural)</i> memoirs, reminiscences, memorials</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>вос<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ми.html>ми</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>вос-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-помин-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-ниj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восприимчивость.html>восприи́мчивость</a> (27660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">восприи́мчивый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vospriímčivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***воспринимать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воспринимать.html>воспринима́ть</a> (3771)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспринимать.html>воспринима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosprinimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспринять.html>восприня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to perceive, to apprehend</li>
<li>to appreciate, to take in <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to be aware of</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воспроизвести.html>воспроизвести́</a> (12943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вос-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vos-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произвести.html>произвести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proizvestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспроизвести.html>воспроизвести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosproizvestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспроизводить.html>воспроизводи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to reproduce</li>
<li>to recall, to call to mind</li>
<li>to repeat</li>
<li><i>(tape recorder, VCR etc.)</i> to play <i>(back)</i></li>
<li>to reprint</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вос-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vos-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:производить.html>производи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proizvodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспроизводить.html>воспроизводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosproizvodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспроизвести.html>воспроизвести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to reproduce</li>
<li>to recall, to call to mind</li>
<li>to repeat</li>
<li><i>(tape recorder, VCR etc.)</i> to play <i>(back)</i></li>
<li>to reprint</li></ol>
